<script>
      (function(p) {
        function getCookiesMap(t) {
          return t.split("; ").map(function(t) {
            return t.trim().split(/=(.+)/);
          }).reduce(function(t, i) {
            return t[i[0]] = i[1], t;
          }, {})
        }

        var cookieMap = getCookiesMap(document.cookie);
        var ciCookieMap = {};

        if (getCookiesMap(document.cookie).ci) {
          getCookiesMap(document.cookie).ci.split("&").forEach(function(t) {
            var parts = t.split('=');
            ciCookieMap[parts[0]] = parts[1];
          });
        }

        var regime = ciCookieMap && ciCookieMap['TWC-Privacy'] || 'exempt';

        var privacyPages = ['/en-US/twc/privacy-policy','/es-US/intl-privacy'];

        var isPrivacyPage = privacyPages.some(function(page) {
          return document.location.pathname.indexOf(page) > -1;
        });

        if (regime === 'exempt' && !isPrivacyPage) {
          var element = document.createElement('div');
          element.id = 'teconsent';
          element.className = 'truste-link';

          var truste_country ='US';
          var truste_url = truste_country && 'https://consent.truste.com/notice?domain=weather.com&c=teconsent&country=US' ||
                        'https://consent.truste.com/notice?domain=weather.com&c=teconsent';
          var sb = document.createElement('script');
          sb.src = truste_url;

          element.appendChild(sb)
          p.appendChild(element);
        } else {
          var element = document.createElement('div');
          element.id = "dpr-manager";
          p.appendChild(element);
        }
      })(
        document.getElementById('truste-container')
      )
    </script>
